                      Sá»‘ lÆ°á»£ng: <b>x{qty}</b>
                    </p>
                    {prescriptionUrl && (
                      <a href={prescriptionUrl} target="_blank" rel="noreferrer"
                        style={{ display: "inline-block", marginTop: "6px", fontSize: "13px", color: "#b91c1c", fontWeight: "bold", textDecoration: "underline" }}>
                        ðŸ‘ï¸ Xem Toa thuá»‘c / ÄÆ¡n kÃ­nh
                      </a>

                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontWeight: "bold", fontSize: "16px", color: "#059669", whiteSpace: "nowrap" }}>
                    {formatUSD(unitPrice)}

        {/* Tá»•ng cá»™ng */}
        <div style={{ textAlign: "right", fontSize: "20px", backgroundColor: "#f0fdf4", padding: "16px 20px", borderRadius: "8px", border: "1px solid #bbf7d0" }}>

            {formatUSD(order.totalAmount)}
          </strong>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext } from "react";
import { Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { UserContext } from "../context/UserContext";
import "./OrderHistory.css";

export default function OrderHistory() {
  const { user } = useContext(UserContext);
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const [orders, setOrders] = useState([]);
  const [preorders, setPreorders] = useState([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("all"); // "all" | "orders" | "preorders"

  useEffect(() => {
    const token = user?.token || JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"))?.token;
    if (!token) {
      navigate("/login");
      return;
    }

    const fetchAll = async () => {
      setIsLoading(true);
      setError("");
      try {
        // Gá»i song song cáº£ 2 API
        const [ordersRes, preordersRes] = await Promise.all([
          fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Orders/my?page=1&pageSize=100", {
            headers: {
              "Content-Type": "application/json",
              Accept: "application/json",
              Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
            },
          }),
          fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Preorders/my", {
            headers: {
              "Content-Type": "application/json",
              Accept: "application/json",
              Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
            },
          }),
        ]);

        if (ordersRes.ok) {
          const data = await ordersRes.json();
          setOrders(data.items || data || []);
        } else if (ordersRes.status !== 404) {
          console.warn("Orders API error:", ordersRes.status);
        }

        if (preordersRes.ok) {
          const data = await preordersRes.json();
          setPreorders(data.items || data || []);
        } else if (preordersRes.status !== 404) {
          console.warn("Preorders API error:", preordersRes.status);
        }
      } catch (err) {
        setError("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i. KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ táº£i lá»‹ch sá»­ Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng.");
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    };

    fetchAll();
  }, [user, navigate]);

  const translateStatus = (status) => {
    const s = status?.toLowerCase();
    if (s === "pending") return { text: "Chá» xÃ¡c nháº­n", color: "#f59e0b" };
    if (s === "processing") return { text: "Äang xá»­ lÃ½", color: "#3b82f6" };
    if (s === "shipped" || s === "delivering") return { text: "Äang giao hÃ ng", color: "#8b5cf6" };
    if (s === "delivered" || s === "completed") return { text: "ThÃ nh cÃ´ng", color: "#10b981" };
    if (s === "cancelled") return { text: "ÄÃ£ huá»·", color: "#ef4444" };
    if (s === "awaiting_payment" || s === "awaitingpayment") return { text: "Chá» thanh toÃ¡n", color: "#f97316" };
    return { text: status || "KhÃ´ng rÃµ", color: "gray" };
  };

  const formatDate = (dateStr) => {
    if (!dateStr) return "â€”";
    return new Date(dateStr).toLocaleDateString("vi-VN");
  };

  // Sáº¯p xáº¿p theo ngÃ y má»›i nháº¥t
  const sortedOrders = [...orders].sort(
    (a, b) => new Date(b.orderDate || b.createdAt || 0) - new Date(a.orderDate || a.createdAt || 0)
  );
  const sortedPreorders = [...preorders].sort(
    (a, b) => new Date(b.createdAt || b.orderDate || 0) - new Date(a.createdAt || a.orderDate || 0)
  );

  const tabStyle = (tab) => ({
    padding: "10px 24px",
    borderRadius: "8px 8px 0 0",
    border: "none",
    cursor: "pointer",
    fontWeight: "bold",
    fontSize: "15px",
    backgroundColor: activeTab === tab ? "white" : "#f3f4f6",
    color: activeTab === tab ? "#111827" : "#6b7280",
    borderBottom: activeTab === tab ? "3px solid #2563eb" : "3px solid transparent",
    transition: "all 0.2s",
  });

  // Render má»™t card Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng thÆ°á»ng
  const OrderCard = ({ order }) => {
    const statusObj = translateStatus(order.status);
    const itemsList = order.orderDetails || order.orderItems || order.items || [];
    const totalQty =
      order.totalQuantity ||
      order.totalItems ||
      itemsList.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.quantity || item.qty || 1), 0);

    return (
      <div
        style={{
          marginBottom: "16px",
          border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
          borderRadius: "10px",
          padding: "20px",
          backgroundColor: "white",
          boxShadow: "0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,0.05)",
        }}
      >
        <div
          style={{
            display: "flex",
            justifyContent: "space-between",
            borderBottom: "1px solid #f3f4f6",
            paddingBottom: "12px",
            marginBottom: "12px",
            flexWrap: "wrap",
            gap: "8px",
          }}
        >
          <div>
            <p style={{ margin: "0 0 4px 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#6b7280" }}>
              <b>MÃ£ Ä‘Æ¡n:</b> #{order.id || order.orderId}
            </p>
            <p style={{ margin: 0, fontWeight: "bold", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              NgÃ y Ä‘áº·t: {formatDate(order.orderDate || order.createdAt)}
            </p>
          </div>
          <span
            style={{
              fontWeight: "bold",
              color: statusObj.color,
              backgroundColor: `${statusObj.color}18`,
              padding: "5px 14px",
              borderRadius: "20px",
              fontSize: "13px",
              alignSelf: "flex-start",
            }}
          >
            {statusObj.text}
          </span>
        </div>

        <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: "10px" }}>
          <div>
            <p style={{ margin: "0 0 4px 0" }}>
              Tá»•ng tiá»n:{" "}
              <strong style={{ color: "#111827", fontSize: "18px" }}>
                ${order.totalAmount || order.totalPrice || 0}
              </strong>
            </p>
            <p style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: "13px", color: "#6b7280" }}>
              Sá»‘ sáº£n pháº©m: <b>{totalQty}</b>
            </p>
          </div>
          <Link
            to={`/orders/${order.id || order.orderId}`}
            style={{
              padding: "8px 18px",
              border: "1px solid #d1d5db",
              borderRadius: "6px",
              textDecoration: "none",
              color: "#111827",
              fontWeight: "500",
              fontSize: "14px",
              backgroundColor: "#f9fafb",
            }}
          >
            Xem chi tiáº¿t â†’
          </Link>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // Render má»™t card Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c (PRE-ORDER)
  const PreorderCard = ({ order }) => {
    const statusObj = translateStatus(order.status);
    const itemsList = order.preorderDetails || order.items || [];
    const totalQty = itemsList.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.quantity || 1), 0);
    
    // State lÆ°u tá»•ng tiá»n Ä‘á»ƒ cÃ³ thá»ƒ update báº¥t Ä‘á»“ng bá»™
    const [finalAmount, setFinalAmount] = useState(
      order.totalAmount || order.totalPrice ||
      itemsList.reduce((sum, item) => {
        const itemPrice = item.unitPrice || item.price || 0;
        const itemQty = item.quantity || item.qty || 1;
        return sum + (itemPrice * itemQty);
      }, 0)
    );

    // âš¡ FIX: Náº¿u tá»•ng tiá»n váº«n báº±ng 0 (do BE thiáº¿u data), gá»i API Payment Ä‘á»ƒ láº¥y sá»‘ tiá»n Ä‘Ã£ tráº£
    useEffect(() => {
      const fetchPaymentAmount = async () => {
        if (finalAmount === 0 || !finalAmount) {
          try {
            const token = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"))?.token;
            const preId = order.id || order.preorderId;
            const res = await fetch(`https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Payments/preorder/${preId}`, {
              headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` }
            });
            if (res.ok) {
              const data = await res.json();
              // API cÃ³ thá»ƒ tráº£ vá» 1 máº£ng cÃ¡c payment hoáº·c 1 object, ta láº¥y amount
              if (data && data.length > 0 && data[0].amount) {
                setFinalAmount(data[0].amount);
              } else if (data && data.amount) {
                setFinalAmount(data.amount);
              }
            }
          } catch (err) {
            console.error("Lá»—i láº¥y thÃ´ng tin Payment:", err);
          }
        }
      };

      fetchPaymentAmount();
    }, [order, finalAmount]);

    return (
      <div
        style={{
          marginBottom: "16px",
          border: "1px solid #bfdbfe",
          borderRadius: "10px",
          padding: "20px",
          backgroundColor: "#eff6ff",
          boxShadow: "0 1px 4px rgba(37,99,235,0.08)",
        }}
      >
        {/* Badge PRE-ORDER */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: "10px" }}>
          <span
            style={{
              backgroundColor: "#2563eb",
              color: "white",
              fontSize: "11px",
              fontWeight: "bold",
              padding: "3px 10px",
              borderRadius: "20px",
              letterSpacing: "0.5px",
            }}
          >
            ðŸš€ PRE-ORDER
          </span>
        </div>

        <div
          style={{
            display: "flex",
            justifyContent: "space-between",
            borderBottom: "1px solid #dbeafe",
            paddingBottom: "12px",
            marginBottom: "12px",
            flexWrap: "wrap",
            gap: "8px",
          }}
        >
          <div>
            <p style={{ margin: "0 0 4px 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#1e40af" }}>
              <b>MÃ£ Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c:</b> #{order.id || order.preorderId}
            </p>
            <p style={{ margin: 0, fontWeight: "bold", fontSize: "14px", color: "#1e3a8a" }}>
              NgÃ y Ä‘áº·t: {formatDate(order.createdAt || order.orderDate)}
            </p>
            {order.expectedDate && (
              <p style={{ margin: "4px 0 0 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#1d4ed8" }}>
                ðŸ“… Dá»± kiáº¿n giao: {formatDate(order.expectedDate)}
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          <span
            style={{
              fontWeight: "bold",
              color: statusObj.color,
              backgroundColor: `${statusObj.color}18`,
              padding: "5px 14px",
              borderRadius: "20px",

            }}
          >

              Tá»•ng tiá»n:{" "}

              <strong style={{ color: "#1e40af", fontSize: "18px" }}>
                ${finalAmount}
              </strong>
            </p>
            {totalQty > 0 && (
              <p style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: "13px", color: "#1e40af" }}>

             to={`/preorders/${order.id || order.preorderId}`}

            }}

              Báº¯t Ä‘áº§u mua sáº¯m
            </Link>
          </div>
        )}

        {!isLoading && (
          <>
            {/* TAB: Táº¤T Cáº¢ */}
            {activeTab === "all" && (
              <>
                {sortedPreorders.map((order) => (
                  <PreorderCard key={`pre-${order.id || order.preorderId}`} order={order} />
                ))}
                {sortedOrders.map((order) => (
                  <OrderCard key={`ord-${order.id || order.orderId}`} order={order} />
                ))}
                {totalCount === 0 && !error && (
                  <p style={{ textAlign: "center", color: "#6b7280" }}>ChÆ°a cÃ³ Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng nÃ o.</p>
                )}
              </>
            )}

            {/* TAB: ÄÆ N THÆ¯á»œNG */}
            {activeTab === "orders" && (
              <>
                {sortedOrders.length === 0 ? (
                  <p style={{ textAlign: "center", color: "#6b7280", padding: "30px 0" }}>
                    ChÆ°a cÃ³ Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng thÆ°á»ng nÃ o.
                  </p>
                ) : (
                  sortedOrders.map((order) => (
                    <OrderCard key={order.id || order.orderId} order={order} />
                  ))
                )}
              </>
            )}

            {/* TAB: Äáº¶T TRÆ¯á»šC */}
            {activeTab === "preorders" && (
              <>
                {sortedPreorders.length === 0 ? (
                  <p style={{ textAlign: "center", color: "#6b7280", padding: "30px 0" }}>
                    ChÆ°a cÃ³ Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c nÃ o.
                  </p>
                ) : (
                  sortedPreorders.map((order) => (
                    <PreorderCard key={order.id || order.preorderId} order={order} />
                  ))
                )}
              </>
            )}
          </>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext } from "react";
import { useParams, Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { UserContext } from "../context/UserContext";

export default function PreorderDetail() {
  const { id } = useParams();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { user } = useContext(UserContext);
  const [order, setOrder] = useState(null);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  useEffect(() => {
    const token = user?.token || JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"))?.token;
    if (!token) { navigate("/login"); return; }

    const fetchDetail = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Preorders/${id}`, {
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` },
        });
        if (res.ok) {
          const data = await res.json();

          // ===== DEBUG: TÃ¬m field Ä‘á»‹a chá»‰ trong preorder response =====
          console.log("PREORDER DETAIL - Táº¤T Cáº¢ FIELDS:");
          const topLevelFields = {};
          Object.entries(data).forEach(([k, v]) => {
            if (typeof v !== "object" || v === null) topLevelFields[k] = v;
          });
          console.table(topLevelFields);
          if (data.user) {
            console.log("ðŸ‘¤ user object:", data.user);
          }
          // =============================================================

          setOrder(data);
        } else if (res.status === 404) {
          setError("KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c nÃ y.");
        } else {
          setError(`Lá»—i ${res.status} khi táº£i chi tiáº¿t.`);
        }
      } catch {
        setError("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i. Vui lÃ²ng thá»­ láº¡i.");
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    };
    fetchDetail();
  }, [id, user, navigate]);

  if (isLoading)
    return <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "60px", color: "#666" }}>Äang táº£i chi tiáº¿t Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c...</div>;

  if (error || !order)
    return (
      <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "60px" }}>
        <h2 style={{ color: "#dc2626" }}>{error || "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c"}</h2>
        <Link to="/orders" style={{ color: "#3b82f6" }}>â† Quay láº¡i lá»‹ch sá»­ mua hÃ ng</Link>
      </div>
    );

  const formatUSD = (n) =>
    new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US", { style: "currency", currency: "USD", minimumFractionDigits: 0 }).format(n || 0);

  const formatDate = (d) => d ? new Date(d).toLocaleString("vi-VN") : "â€”";

  const getStatusBadge = (status) => {
    const s = status?.toLowerCase() || "";
    const map = {
      pending:          { text: "Chá» xÃ¡c nháº­n",   color: "#d97706", bg: "#fef3c7" },
      confirmed:        { text: "ÄÃ£ xÃ¡c nháº­n",    color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      processing:       { text: "Äang xá»­ lÃ½",     color: "#4338ca", bg: "#ede9fe" },
      awaiting_payment: { text: "Chá» thanh toÃ¡n", color: "#f97316", bg: "#fff7ed" },
      awaitingpayment:  { text: "Chá» thanh toÃ¡n", color: "#f97316", bg: "#fff7ed" },
      paid:             { text: "ÄÃ£ thanh toÃ¡n",  color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      shipped:          { text: "Äang giao hÃ ng", color: "#7e22ce", bg: "#f3e8ff" },
      delivered:        { text: "HoÃ n thÃ nh",     color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      completed:        { text: "HoÃ n thÃ nh",     color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      cancelled:        { text: "ÄÃ£ huá»·",         color: "#dc2626", bg: "#fee2e2" },
    };
    const s2 = map[s] || { text: status || "KhÃ´ng rÃµ", color: "#6b7280", bg: "#f3f4f6" };
    return (

        {s2.text}
      </span>
    );
  };

  const receiverPhone = order.user?.phone    || "â€”";

    order.shippingAddress  ||

    order.address          ||

import React, { useState, useContext } from "react"; 
import { Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { UserContext } from "../context/UserContext"; 
import { GoogleLogin } from "@react-oauth/google"; 
import "./Auth.css";

export default function RegisterPage() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { login } = useContext(UserContext); 
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({ fullName: "", email: "", phone: "", password: "", confirmPassword: "" });
  const [errorMsg, setErrorMsg] = useState("");
  const [successMsg, setSuccessMsg] = useState("");
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleChange = (e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [e.target.name]: e.target.value }));

  const handleRegister = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setErrorMsg(""); setSuccessMsg("");
    
    if (formData.password !== formData.confirmPassword) { 
      setErrorMsg("Máº­t kháº©u xÃ¡c nháº­n khÃ´ng khá»›p!"); 
      return; 
    }
    
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const response = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Auth/register", {
        method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ 
          email: formData.email, 
          password: formData.password, 
          fullName: formData.fullName, 
          phone: formData.phone 
        }),
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      
      if (response.ok || response.status === 201) {
        // âš¡ Tá»° Äá»˜NG ÄÄ‚NG NHáº¬P SAU KHI ÄÄ‚NG KÃ THÃ€NH CÃ”NG
        login({ 
          token: data.token, 
          userId: data.userId, 
          email: data.email, 
          fullName: data.fullName, 
          role: data.role 
        });
        setSuccessMsg("ÄÄƒng kÃ½ thÃ nh cÃ´ng! Äang chuyá»ƒn hÆ°á»›ng...");
        setTimeout(() => navigate("/"), 2000);
      } else { 
        setErrorMsg(data.message || "ÄÄƒng kÃ½ tháº¥t báº¡i!"); 
      }
    } catch (error) { 
      setErrorMsg("KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ káº¿t ná»‘i Ä‘áº¿n Server."); 
    } finally { 
      setIsLoading(false); 
    }
  };

  const handleGoogleSuccess = async (credentialResponse) => {
    setIsLoading(true); setErrorMsg("");
    try {
      const response = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Auth/google", {
        method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ idToken: credentialResponse.credential }),
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      if (response.ok) {
        // âš¡ ÄÄ‚NG NHáº¬P GOOGLE Tá»ª TRANG ÄÄ‚NG KÃ
        login({ 
          token: data.token, 
          userId: data.userId, 
          email: data.email, 
          fullName: data.fullName, 
          role: data.role 
        });
        navigate("/");
      } else { 
        setErrorMsg("XÃ¡c thá»±c Google tháº¥t báº¡i!"); 
      }
    } catch (error) { 
      setErrorMsg("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i API Google."); 
    } finally { 
      setIsLoading(false); 
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="auth-container register-container">
      <h2 className="auth-title">ÄÄƒng KÃ½ TÃ i Khoáº£n</h2>
      
      {errorMsg && <div className="auth-msg error">{errorMsg}</div>}
      {successMsg && <div className="auth-msg success">{successMsg}</div>}

      <form onSubmit={handleRegister} className="auth-form">
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Há» vÃ  TÃªn:</label>
          <input type="text" name="fullName" value={formData.fullName} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p há» vÃ  tÃªn" />
        </div>
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Email:</label>
          <input type="email" name="email" value={formData.email} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p email" />
        </div>
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Sá»‘ Ä‘iá»‡n thoáº¡i:</label>
          <input type="tel" name="phone" value={formData.phone} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p sá»‘ Ä‘iá»‡n thoáº¡i" />
        </div>
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Máº­t kháº©u:</label>
          <input type="password" name="password" value={formData.password} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p máº­t kháº©u" />
        </div>
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>XÃ¡c nháº­n máº­t kháº©u:</label>
          <input type="password" name="confirmPassword" value={formData.confirmPassword} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p láº¡i máº­t kháº©u" />
        </div>

        <button type="submit" disabled={isLoading} className="btn-submit">
          {isLoading ? "Äang xá»­ lÃ½..." : "ÄÄƒng KÃ½"}
        </button>
      </form>

      <div className="auth-divider">
        <div className="line"></div><span className="text">HOáº¶C</span><div className="line"></div>
      </div>

      <div className="auth-google-btn">
        <GoogleLogin onSuccess={handleGoogleSuccess} onError={() => setErrorMsg("ÄÄƒng kÃ½ Google tháº¥t báº¡i")} shape="pill" theme="outline" text="signup_with" />
      </div>

      <div className="auth-footer">
        ÄÃ£ cÃ³ tÃ i khoáº£n? <Link to="/login" className="auth-link">ÄÄƒng nháº­p ngay</Link>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext } from 'react';
import { UserContext } from '../context/UserContext';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import './UserProfile.css';

export default function UserProfile() {
  const { user } = useContext(UserContext);
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("info");
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState(null);
  const [editMode, setEditMode] = useState(false);
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({ fullName: '', phone: '', address: '' });
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);

  
  const [prescriptions, setPrescriptions] = useState([]);
  const [isAddingPrescription, setIsAddingPrescription] = useState(false);
  const [prescriptionForm, setPrescriptionForm] = useState({
    sphereRight: 0, cylinderRight: 0, axisRight: 0, addRight: 0,
    sphereLeft: 0, cylinderLeft: 0, axisLeft: 0, addLeft: 0,
    pupillaryDistance: 60, doctorName: "", clinicName: ""
  });

  const token = user?.token || JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"))?.token;

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!token) {
      navigate('/login');
      return;
    }
    fetchProfile();
    fetchPrescriptions(); 
  }, [token, navigate]);

  const fetchProfile = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Users/me", {
        headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` }
      });
      if (res.ok) {
        const data = await res.json();
        setProfile(data);
        setFormData({ fullName: data.fullName || '', phone: data.phone || '', address: data.address || '' });
      }
    } catch (err) { console.error("Lá»—i profile"); } 
    finally { setIsLoading(false); }
  };

  
  const fetchPrescriptions = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Prescriptions/my?page=1&pageSize=10", {
        headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` }
      });
      if (res.ok) {
        const data = await res.json();
        setPrescriptions(data.items || data || []);
      }
    } catch (err) { console.error("Lá»—i láº¥y toa thuá»‘c"); }
  };

  const handleUpdateProfile = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    try {
      const res = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Users/me", {
        method: "PUT",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` },
        body: JSON.stringify(formData)
      });
      if (res.ok) {
        alert("Cáº­p nháº­t thÃ nh cÃ´ng!");
        setEditMode(false);
        fetchProfile();
      }
    } catch (err) { alert("Lá»—i khi cáº­p nháº­t"); }
  };

  
 const handleSavePrescription = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    
    const expiryDate = new Date();
    expiryDate.setMonth(expiryDate.getMonth() + 6);

    // âš¡ Xá»¬ LÃ Lá»–I VALIDATION: DÃ¹ng null náº¿u khÃ´ng cÃ³ giÃ¡ trá»‹ thay vÃ¬ dÃ¹ng 0
    const payload = {
      sphereRight: prescriptionForm.sphereRight ? Number(prescriptionForm.sphereRight) : null,
      cylinderRight: prescriptionForm.cylinderRight ? Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderRight) : null,
      axisRight: prescriptionForm.axisRight ? Number(prescriptionForm.axisRight) : null,
      addRight: prescriptionForm.addRight ? Number(prescriptionForm.addRight) : null,
      
      sphereLeft: prescriptionForm.sphereLeft ? Number(prescriptionForm.sphereLeft) : null,
      cylinderLeft: prescriptionForm.cylinderLeft ? Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderLeft) : null,
      axisLeft: prescriptionForm.axisLeft ? Number(prescriptionForm.axisLeft) : null,
      addLeft: prescriptionForm.addLeft ? Number(prescriptionForm.addLeft) : null,
      
      pupillaryDistance: prescriptionForm.pupillaryDistance ? Number(prescriptionForm.pupillaryDistance) : 60,
      doctorName: prescriptionForm.doctorName || "KhÃ¡ch tá»± nháº­p",
      clinicName: prescriptionForm.clinicName || "KhÃ¡ch tá»± nháº­p",
      expirationDate: expiryDate.toISOString()
    };

    try {
      const res = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Prescriptions", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` },
        body: JSON.stringify(payload)
      });
      
      if (res.ok) {
        alert("ÄÃ£ lÆ°u toa thuá»‘c thÃ nh cÃ´ng!");
        setIsAddingPrescription(false);
        fetchPrescriptions(); 
      } else {
        const err = await res.json(); // Äá»c dáº¡ng JSON Ä‘á»ƒ bÃ¡o lá»—i cá»¥ thá»ƒ
        alert("Lá»—i nháº­p liá»‡u: " + (err.message || "Kiá»ƒm tra láº¡i cÃ¡c thÃ´ng sá»‘."));
      }
    } catch (err) {
      alert("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i.");
    }
  };

  if (isLoading) return <div style={{textAlign: 'center', padding: '50px'}}>Äang táº£i...</div>;

  return (
    <div className="profile-container" style={{maxWidth: '800px', margin: '40px auto', padding: '20px', fontFamily: 'sans-serif'}}>
      <h2 style={{borderBottom: '2px solid #000', paddingBottom: '10px'}}>Quáº£n LÃ½ TÃ i Khoáº£n</h2>
      
      <div style={{display: 'flex', gap: '20px', marginBottom: '20px'}}>
        <button onClick={() => setActiveTab("info")} style={{padding: '10px 20px', fontWeight: 'bold', background: activeTab === 'info' ? '#000' : '#f3f4f6', color: activeTab === 'info' ? '#fff' : '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer'}}>ThÃ´ng tin cÃ¡ nhÃ¢n</button>
        <button onClick={() => setActiveTab("prescription")} style={{padding: '10px 20px', fontWeight: 'bold', background: activeTab === 'prescription' ? '#000' : '#f3f4f6', color: activeTab === 'prescription' ? '#fff' : '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer'}}>Toa thuá»‘c cá»§a tÃ´i</button>
      </div>

      
      {activeTab === "info" && (
        <div style={{background: '#f9fafb', padding: '20px', borderRadius: '8px'}}>
          {!editMode ? (
            <div>
              <p><b>Há» vÃ  tÃªn:</b> {profile?.fullName}</p>
              <p><b>Email:</b> {profile?.email}</p>
              <p><b>Sá»‘ Ä‘iá»‡n thoáº¡i:</b> {profile?.phone || 'ChÆ°a cáº­p nháº­t'}</p>
              <p><b>Äá»‹a chá»‰:</b> {profile?.address || 'ChÆ°a cáº­p nháº­t'}</p>
              <button onClick={() => setEditMode(true)} style={{marginTop: '15px', padding: '10px 20px', background: '#3b82f6', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer'}}>Sá»­a ThÃ´ng Tin</button>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <form onSubmit={handleUpdateProfile} style={{display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '15px'}}>

import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { useSearchParams, Link } from "react-router-dom";

export default function VNPayReturnPage() {
  const [searchParams] = useSearchParams();
  const [status, setStatus] = useState("loading");

  // Backend redirect vá» vá»›i cÃ¡c params nÃ y
  const responseCode = searchParams.get("vnp_ResponseCode");
  const transactionNo = searchParams.get("vnp_TransactionNo") || searchParams.get("transactionId");
  const amount = searchParams.get("vnp_Amount") || searchParams.get("amount");
  const message = searchParams.get("message"); // Backend cÃ³ thá»ƒ gá»­i thÃªm "message"
  const paymentId = searchParams.get("paymentId");

  useEffect(() => {
  

    // Debug: in ra params Ä‘á»ƒ kiá»ƒm tra
    console.log("ðŸ”µ VNPay Return Params:", {
      responseCode,
      transactionNo,
      amount,
      message,
      paymentId,
      fullUrl: window.location.search,
    });

    // responseCode "00" = thÃ nh cÃ´ng (chuáº©n VNPay)
    // Má»™t sá»‘ backend tá»± custom redirect vá»›i params riÃªng
    if (responseCode === "00") {
      setStatus("success");
    } else if (responseCode) {
      // CÃ³ responseCode nhÆ°ng khÃ´ng pháº£i "00"
      setStatus("failed");
    } else if (message) {
      
      const isSuccess =
        message.toLowerCase().includes("success") ||
        message.toLowerCase().includes("thÃ nh cÃ´ng");
      setStatus(isSuccess ? "success" : "failed");
    } else {
      // KhÃ´ng cÃ³ params gÃ¬ háº¿t â†’ lá»—i
      setStatus("failed");
    }
  }, [responseCode, message]);

  const formatAmount = (raw) => {
    if (!raw) return "â€”";
    // VNPay tráº£ amount * 100, backend cÃ³ thá»ƒ Ä‘Ã£ chia rá»“i
    const num = Number(raw);
    if (num > 1_000_000) {
      // ChÆ°a chia â€” chia 100 Ä‘á»ƒ ra VND thá»±c
      return new Intl.NumberFormat("vi-VN", {
        style: "currency",
        currency: "VND",
      }).format(num / 100);
    }
    return new Intl.NumberFormat("vi-VN", {
      style: "currency",
      currency: "VND",
    }).format(num);
  };

  return (
    <div
      style={{
        textAlign: "center",
        padding: "80px 20px",
        fontFamily: "sans-serif",
        minHeight: "60vh",
        display: "flex",
        alignItems: "center",
        justifyContent: "center",
      }}
    >
      {/* LOADING */}
      {status === "loading" && (
        <div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: "50px", marginBottom: "16px" }}>â³</div>
          <h2 style={{ color: "#6b7280" }}>Äang kiá»ƒm tra káº¿t quáº£ thanh toÃ¡n...</h2>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* THÃ€NH CÃ”NG */}
      {status === "success" && (
        <div
          style={{
            backgroundColor: "#f0fdf4",
            maxWidth: "500px",
            width: "100%",
            margin: "0 auto",
            padding: "40px 30px",
            borderRadius: "16px",
            border: "1px solid #bbf7d0",
            boxShadow: "0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.08)",
          }}
        >
          <div style={{ fontSize: "64px" }}>âœ…</div>
          <h2 style={{ color: "#059669", marginTop: "12px", fontSize: "24px" }}>
            Thanh ToÃ¡n VNPay ThÃ nh CÃ´ng!
          </h2>
          <p style={{ color: "#374151", marginTop: "8px" }}>
            Cáº£m Æ¡n báº¡n! ÄÆ¡n hÃ ng cá»§a báº¡n Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Æ°á»£c ghi nháº­n.
          </p>

          <div
            style={{
              textAlign: "left",
              backgroundColor: "white",
              padding: "16px",
              borderRadius: "10px",
              marginTop: "20px",
              border: "1px solid #d1fae5",
            }}
          >
            {transactionNo && (
              <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", color: "#374151", fontSize: "14px" }}>
                <b>MÃ£ giao dá»‹ch:</b> {transactionNo}
              </p>
            )}
            {paymentId && (
              <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", color: "#374151", fontSize: "14px" }}>
                <b>Payment ID:</b> {paymentId}
              </p>
            )}
            {amount && (
              <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", color: "#374151", fontSize: "14px" }}>
                <b>Sá»‘ tiá»n:</b> {formatAmount(amount)}
              </p>
            )}
          </div>

          <div
            style={{ display: "flex", gap: "12px", marginTop: "24px", justifyContent: "center" }}
          >
            <Link
              to="/orders"
              style={{
                display: "inline-block",
                padding: "12px 24px",
                backgroundColor: "#059669",
                color: "white",
                textDecoration: "none",
                borderRadius: "8px",
                fontWeight: "bold",
                fontSize: "15px",
              }}
            >
              Xem Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng
            </Link>
            <Link
              to="/"
              style={{
                display: "inline-block",
                padding: "12px 24px",
                backgroundColor: "#111827",
                color: "white",
                textDecoration: "none",
                borderRadius: "8px",
                fontWeight: "bold",
                fontSize: "15px",
              }}
            >
              Vá» trang chá»§
            </Link>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* THáº¤T Báº I */}
      {status === "failed" && (
        <div
          style={{
            backgroundColor: "#fef2f2",
            maxWidth: "500px",
            width: "100%",
            margin: "0 auto",
            padding: "40px 30px",

            boxShadow: "0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.08)",
          }}
        >
          <div style={{ fontSize: "64px" }}>âŒ</div>
          <h2 style={{ color: "#dc2626", marginTop: "12px", fontSize: "24px" }}>
            Thanh ToÃ¡n Tháº¥t Báº¡i
          </h2>
          <p style={{ color: "#374151", marginTop: "8px" }}>
            Giao dá»‹ch chÆ°a Ä‘Æ°á»£c hoÃ n táº¥t. ÄÆ¡n hÃ ng váº«n Ä‘Æ°á»£c lÆ°u â€” báº¡n cÃ³ thá»ƒ thá»­ thanh toÃ¡n láº¡i.
          </p>

          {/* Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ lÃ½ do tháº¥t báº¡i náº¿u cÃ³ */}
          {(responseCode || message) && (
            <div
              style={{
                textAlign: "left",
                backgroundColor: "white",
                padding: "12px 16px",
                borderRadius: "8px",
                marginTop: "16px",
                border: "1px solid #fecaca",
              }}
            >
              {responseCode && responseCode !== "00" && (
                <p style={{ margin: "4px 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#6b7280" }}>
                  <b>MÃ£ lá»—i VNPay:</b> {responseCode}
                </p>
              )}
              {message && (
                <p style={{ margin: "4px 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#6b7280" }}>
                  <b>Chi tiáº¿t:</b> {decodeURIComponent(message)}
                </p>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          <div
            style={{ display: "flex", gap: "12px", marginTop: "24px", justifyContent: "center" }}
          >
            <Link
              to="/orders"
              style={{
                display: "inline-block",
                padding: "12px 24px",
                backgroundColor: "#dc2626",
                color: "white",
                textDecoration: "none",
                borderRadius: "8px",
                fontWeight: "bold",
                fontSize: "15px",
              }}
            >
              Xem Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng
            </Link>
            <Link
              to="/"

                display: "inline-block",
                padding: "12px 24px",
                backgroundColor: "#6b7280",

            >
              Vá» trang chá»§
            </Link>

FILE: routes\AdminProtectedRoute.jsx

import React, { useContext } from 'react';
import { Navigate, Outlet } from 'react-router-dom';
import { UserContext } from '../context/UserContext';

export default function AdminProtectedRoute() {
  const { user } = useContext(UserContext);

  // Láº¥y role tá»« user context (chuáº©n chá»¯ thÆ°á»ng)
  const role = user?.role || "";

  // Cho phÃ©p admin, manager vÃ  staff vÃ o khu vá»±c quáº£n trá»‹ chung.
  if (role !== "admin" && role !== "manager" && role !== "staff") {
    return <Navigate to="/" replace />;
  }
  
  return <Outlet />;
}

    <>
      <Header />
      <main style={{ minHeight: '60vh' }}>
        <Outlet /> 
      </main>
      <Footer />
    </>
  );
};

export default function AppRouter() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Routes>
        
        {/* --- ROUTES DÃ€NH CHO ADMIN & STAFF --- */}
        <Route element={<AdminProtectedRoute />}>
          <Route path="/admin" element={<AdminLayout />}>
            <Route index element={<AdminDashboard />} /> 
            <Route path="products" element={<AdminProducts />} />
            <Route path="lenstypes" element={<AdminLensTypes />} />
            <Route path="lensfeatures" element={<AdminLensFeatures />} />
            <Route path="orders" element={<AdminOrders />} />
            <Route path="users" element={<AdminUsers />} />
          </Route>
        </Route>

        {/* --- ROUTES DÃ€NH CHO KHÃCH HÃ€NG CHUNG --- */}
        <Route element={<CustomerLayout />}>
          <Route path="/" element={<MainPage />} />
          <Route path="/products/:id" element={<ProductDetail />} />
          
          <Route path="/orders" element={<OrderHistory />} />
          <Route path="/preorders/:id" element={<PreorderDetail />} />
          <Route path="/orders/:id" element={<OrderDetail />} />

          <Route path="/cart" element={<CartPage />} />
          <Route path="/checkout" element={<CheckoutPage />} />
          
          
          <Route path="/checkout-preorder" element={<CheckoutPreorderPage />} />

          <Route path="/checkout-success" element={<CheckoutSuccess />} />
          <Route path="/payment/return" element={<VNPayReturnPage />} />

          <Route path="/login" element={<LoginPage />} />
          <Route path="/register" element={<RegisterPage />} />
          <Route path="/profile" element={<UserProfile />} />
        </Route>

      </Routes>
    </Router>
  );
}

import React from "react";
import AppRouter from "./routes/AppRouter";
import { CartProvider } from "./context/CartContext";
import { OrderProvider } from "./context/OrderContext"; 
import { UserProvider } from "./context/UserContext"; 

function App() {
  return (
    <UserProvider>  
      <OrderProvider>
        <CartProvider>
          <AppRouter />
        </CartProvider>
      </OrderProvider>
    </UserProvider>
  );
}

export default App;
